07/02/2015 00:00:21 [debug]: sql :select distinct dv.doctor_id,dl.name doctor_name,d.is_general,sl.name specialist
		,dv.price,dv.web_price,
		ifnull(dvv.service_level,4) service_level, ifnull(dvv.pro_level,4) pro_level, ifnull(dvv.facility_level,4) facility_level
		, ifnull(dvv.totle_score,4) totle_score
		 from dr_tb_doctor_vaccine dv 
inner join dr_tb_doctor d on dv.doctor_id=d.id and d.status='A'
left join dr_tb_doctor_lang dl on d.id=dl.oid and dl.lang='zh-cn'
left join dr_tb_doctor_value dvv on d.id=dvv.doctor_id
left join dr_tb_specialist_lang sl on d.specialist_id=sl.oid and sl.lang='zh-cn'
where dv.status='A' and dv.vaccine_id=1 
order by totle_score

	left join dr_tb_vaccine_value ov on o.id=ov.vaccine_id
	where o.id in (1,2) and o.status='A'
	order by booking_count
	limit 0,2

	left join dr_tb_vaccine_value ov on o.id=ov.vaccine_id
	where o.id in (1,2) and o.status='A'
	order by booking_count
	limit 0,2

	left join dr_tb_vaccine_value ov on o.id=ov.vaccine_id
	where o.id in (1,2) and o.status='A'
	order by booking_count
	limit 0,2

	left join dr_tb_vaccine_value ov on o.id=ov.vaccine_id
	where o.id in (1,2) and o.status='A'
	order by booking_count
	limit 0,2

	left join dr_tb_vaccine_value ov on o.id=ov.vaccine_id
	where o.id in (1,2) and o.status='A'
	order by booking_count
	limit 0,2

	where o.id in (1,2) and o.status='A'
	order by booking_count
	limit 0,2

left join dr_tb_vaccine_lang ol on o.id=ol.oid and ol.lang='zh-cn'
	left join dr_tb_vaccine_value ov on o.id=ov.vaccine_id
	where o.id in (1,2) and o.status='A'
	order by booking_count
	limit 0,2
